	jal increment
	lui $2, 40107
	ori $2, $2, 21006
	lui $3, 47302
	ori $3, $3, 2461
	srav $18, $2, $3

 jal init_cp
j breaks

breaks:
	break
 j end

load_patterns:
	lw $15, 0($30)
	lw $16, 4($30)
	jr $31

reset_offsets:
	lui $30, 1
	ori $30, $30, 8
	xor $27, $27, $27
	xor $18, $18, $18
	jr $31

increment_offset:
	addi $30, $30, 8
	addi $27, $27, 2
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

increment_immediate:
	addi $30, $30, 8
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

increment:
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

store:
	sw $18, 0($29)
	sw $19, 0($29)
	jr $31

init_cp:
	mtc0 $0, $12
	mtc0 $0, $13
	mtc0 $0, $14
	mtc0 $0, $15
	jr $31

end:
	 j end
